When this bit is reset, the MAC receiver enables filtering or matching for C-VLAN (Type = 0x8100) packets. RW 0x0 DOVLTC: Disable VLAN Type Comparison This bit is valid only when VLAN Tag Enable of the Filter is set. When this bit is set, the MAC does not check whether the VLAN Tag specified by the Enable Inner VLAN Tag Comparison bit is of type S-VLAN or C-VLAN. When this bit is reset, the MAC filters or matches the VLAN Tag specified by the Enable Inner VLAN Tag Comparison bit only when VLAN Tag type is similar to the one specified by the Enable S-VLAN Match for received Frames bit. RW 0x0 ETV: 12bits or 16bits VLAN comparison This bit is valid only when VEN of the Filter is set. When this bit is set, a 12-bit VLAN identifier is used for comparing and filtering instead of the complete 16-bit VLAN tag. Bits [11:0] of VLAN tag are compared with the corresponding field in the received VLAN-tagged packet. RW 0x0 VEN: VLAN Tag Enable This bit is used to enable or disable the VLAN Tag. When this bit is set, the MAC compares the VLAN Tag of received packet with the VLAN Tag ID. When this bit is reset, no comparison is performed irrespective of the programming of the other fields. 15:0 RW 0x0 VID: VLAN Tag ID This field holds the VLAN Tag value which is used by the MAC for perfect comparison. It is valid when VLAN Tag Enable is set.

1G Ethernet Controller Core Registers EQOS_EQOS_MAC_MAC_VLAN_TAG_FILTER14_0 This register can be accessed only via indirect addressing. The register is added in the spec for informational purpose only. Please refer to databook for details to access this register. This register contains VLAN Tag filter ${i} control information. Offset: 0x700054 Read/Write: See table below Parity Protection: N Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000) Bit R/W Reset Description 31:28 RO 0x0 Reserved_31_y: Reserved. 27:25 RW 0x0 DMACHN: DMA Channel Number The DMA Channel number to which the VLAN Tagged Frame is to be routed if it passes this VLAN Tag Filter is programmed in this field. If the Routing based on VLAN Tag Filter is not necessary, this field need not be programmed. RW 0x0 DMACHEN: DMA Channel Number Enable This bit is the Enable for the DMA Channel Number value programmed in the field DMACH. When this bit is reset, the Routing does not occur based on VLAN Filter result. The frame is routed based on DA Based DMA Channel Routing. 23:21 RO 0x0 Reserved_23_21: Reserved. RW 0x0 ERIVLT: Enable Inner VLAN Tag Comparison This bit is valid only when Double VLAN Tag Enable of the Filter is set. When this bit and the EDVLP field are set, the MAC receiver enables operation on the inner VLAN Tag (if present). When this bit is reset, the MAC receiver enables operation on the outer VLAN Tag (if present). RW 0x0 ERSVLM: Enable S-VLAN Match for received Frames This bit is valid only when VLAN Tag Enable of the Filter is set. When this bit is set, the MAC receiver enables filtering or matching for S-VLAN (Type = 0x88A8) packets. When this bit is reset, the MAC receiver enables filtering or matching for C-VLAN (Type = 0x8100) packets. RW 0x0 DOVLTC: Disable VLAN Type Comparison This bit is valid only when VLAN Tag Enable of the Filter is set. When this bit is set, the MAC does not check whether the VLAN Tag specified by the Enable Inner VLAN Tag Comparison bit is of type S-VLAN or C-VLAN. When this bit is reset, the MAC filters or matches the VLAN Tag specified by the Enable Inner VLAN Tag Comparison bit only when VLAN Tag type is similar to the one specified by the Enable S-VLAN Match for received Frames bit.

RW 0x0 ERSVLM: Enable S-VLAN Match for received Frames This bit is valid only when VLAN Tag Enable of the Filter is set. When this bit is set, the MAC receiver enables filtering or matching for S-VLAN (Type = 0x88A8) packets. When this bit is reset, the MAC receiver enables filtering or matching for C-VLAN (Type = 0x8100) packets. RW 0x0 DOVLTC: Disable VLAN Type Comparison This bit is valid only when VLAN Tag Enable of the Filter is set. When this bit is set, the MAC does not check whether the VLAN Tag specified by the Enable Inner VLAN Tag Comparison bit is of type S-VLAN or C-VLAN. When this bit is reset, the MAC filters or matches the VLAN Tag specified by the Enable Inner VLAN Tag Comparison bit only when VLAN Tag type is similar to the one specified by the Enable S-VLAN Match for received Frames bit.

1G Ethernet Controller Core Registers Bit R/W Reset Description RW 0x0 ETV: 12bits or 16bits VLAN comparison This bit is valid only when VEN of the Filter is set. When this bit is set, a 12-bit VLAN identifier is used for comparing and filtering instead of the complete 16-bit VLAN tag. Bits [11:0] of VLAN tag are compared with the corresponding field in the received VLAN-tagged packet. RW 0x0 VEN: VLAN Tag Enable This bit is used to enable or disable the VLAN Tag. When this bit is set, the MAC compares the VLAN Tag of received packet with the VLAN Tag ID. When this bit is reset, no comparison is performed irrespective of the programming of the other fields. 15:0 RW 0x0 VID: VLAN Tag ID This field holds the VLAN Tag value which is used by the MAC for perfect comparison. It is valid when VLAN Tag Enable is set. EQOS_EQOS_MAC_MAC_VLAN_TAG_FILTER23_0 This register can be accessed only via indirect addressing. The register is added in the spec for informational purpose only. Please refer to databook for details to access this register. This register contains VLAN Tag filter ${i} control information. Offset: 0x1100054 Read/Write: See table below Parity Protection: N Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000) Bit R/W Reset Description 31:28 RO 0x0 Reserved_31_y: Reserved. 27:25 RW 0x0 DMACHN: DMA Channel Number The DMA Channel number to which the VLAN Tagged Frame is to be routed if it passes this VLAN Tag Filter is programmed in this field. If the Routing based on VLAN Tag Filter is not necessary, this field need not be programmed. RW 0x0 DMACHEN: DMA Channel Number Enable This bit is the Enable for the DMA Channel Number value programmed in the field DMACH. When this bit is reset, the Routing does not occur based on VLAN Filter result. The frame is routed based on DA Based DMA Channel Routing. 23:21 RO 0x0 Reserved_23_21: Reserved.

When this bit is reset, the Routing does not occur based on VLAN Filter result. The frame is routed based on DA Based DMA Channel Routing. 23:21 RO 0x0 Reserved_23_21: Reserved.

1G Ethernet Controller Core Registers Bit R/W Reset Description RW 0x0 ERIVLT: Enable Inner VLAN Tag Comparison This bit is valid only when Double VLAN Tag Enable of the Filter is set. When this bit and the EDVLP field are set, the MAC receiver enables operation on the inner VLAN Tag (if present). When this bit is reset, the MAC receiver enables operation on the outer VLAN Tag (if present). RW 0x0 ERSVLM: Enable S-VLAN Match for received Frames This bit is valid only when VLAN Tag Enable of the Filter is set. When this bit is set, the MAC receiver enables filtering or matching for S-VLAN (Type = 0x88A8) packets. When this bit is reset, the MAC receiver enables filtering or matching for C-VLAN (Type = 0x8100) packets. RW 0x0 DOVLTC: Disable VLAN Type Comparison This bit is valid only when VLAN Tag Enable of the Filter is set. When this bit is set, the MAC does not check whether the VLAN Tag specified by the Enable Inner VLAN Tag Comparison bit is of type S-VLAN or C-VLAN. When this bit is reset, the MAC filters or matches the VLAN Tag specified by the Enable Inner VLAN Tag Comparison bit only when VLAN Tag type is similar to the one specified by the Enable S-VLAN Match for received Frames bit. RW 0x0 ETV: 12bits or 16bits VLAN comparison This bit is valid only when VEN of the Filter is set. When this bit is set, a 12-bit VLAN identifier is used for comparing and filtering instead of the complete 16-bit VLAN tag. Bits [11:0] of VLAN tag are compared with the corresponding field in the received VLAN-tagged packet. RW 0x0 VEN: VLAN Tag Enable This bit is used to enable or disable the VLAN Tag. When this bit is set, the MAC compares the VLAN Tag of received packet with the VLAN Tag ID. When this bit is reset, no comparison is performed irrespective of the programming of the other fields. 15:0 RW 0x0 VID: VLAN Tag ID This field holds the VLAN Tag value which is used by the MAC for perfect comparison. It is valid when VLAN Tag Enable is set. EQOS_EQOS_MAC_MAC_VLAN_TAG_FILTER4_0 This register can be accessed only via indirect addressing. The register is added in the spec for informational purpose only. Please refer to databook for details to access this register. This register contains VLAN Tag filter ${i} control information. Offset: 0x1b00054 Read/Write: See table below Parity Protection: N Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000)

Bits[15:13] are the User Priority field, Bit 12 is the CFI/DEI field, and Bits[11:0] are the VID field in the VLAN tag. The following list describes the bits of this field: - Bits[15:13]: User Priority - Bit 12: Canonical Format Indicator (CFI) or Drop Eligible Indicator (DEI) - Bits[11:0]: VLAN Identifier (VID) field of VLAN tag EQOS_EQOS_MAC_MAC_VLAN_INCL6_0 This register can be accessed only via indirect addressing. The register is added in the spec for informational purpose only. Please refer to databook for details to access this register. The Tx Queue ${i} VLAN Tag Inclusion register contains the VLAN tag for insertion in the Transmit packets from Tx Queue ${i}. It also contains the VLAN tag insertion controls. RW 0x0 CSVL: C-VLAN or S-VLAN When this bit is set, S-VLAN type (0x88A8) is inserted in the 13th and 14th bytes of transmitted packets. When this bit is reset, C-VLAN type (0x8100) is inserted in the 13th and 14th bytes of transmitted packets. 18:16 RO 0x0 Reserved_18_16: Reserved. 15:0 RW 0x0 VLT: VLAN Tag for Transmit Packets This field contains the value of the VLAN tag to be inserted. The value must only be changed when the transmit lines are inactive or during the initialization phase. Bits[15:13] are the User Priority field, Bit 12 is the CFI/DEI field, and Bits[11:0] are the VID field in the VLAN tag. The following list describes the bits of this field: - Bits[15:13]: User Priority - Bit 12: Canonical Format Indicator (CFI) or Drop Eligible Indicator (DEI) - Bits[11:0]: VLAN Identifier (VID) field of VLAN tag EQOS_EQOS_MAC_MAC_VLAN_INCL7_0

#### 10.6.4.2 1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers
ETHER_QOS_CLOCK_CTRL_0 Offset: 0x8000 Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0,xxxx,xxx0) Bit Reset Description NORMAL RX_CLK_SEL: NORMAL: RX Clock from the external Ethernet PHY is supplied to CORE LOOPBACK: TX Clock is fed to RX domain to validate LOOPBACK mode 0 = NORMAL 1 = LOOPBACK DISABLE ETHER_QOS_CLK_OVR_ON: SLCG clock overide, Currently only TX & AXI clocks can be SLCGed based on output ports from Synopsys core setting to ENABLE would overide the SLCG enable equation and there by keeps clocks freely oscillating as long as the module clocks are enabled. 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE

1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers ETHER_QOS_AXI_LPI_CTRL_0 Setting to ENABLE is the last resort when enable equation misbehaves, as this setting contributes to power. AXI Low Power Interface Control Programming Guideline to second-level clock gate AXI clock: 1. Program ETHER_QOS_AXI_LPI_CTRL_0.CSYSREQ to 1'b0 to enable AXI clock gating. 2. Poll ETHER_QOS_AXI_LPI_CTRL_0.CSYSACK signal until it is 1'b0. 3. Check the value of ETHER_QOS_AXI_LPI_CTRL_0.CACTIVE, if 1'b1 AXI low power request was not accepted and clock was not gated, if 1'b0, request was accepted and AXI clock was gated internally. 3.a. If CACTIVE was set to 1'b1 in step 3, SW needs to program CSYSREQ to 1'b1 to exit the Low power request before initiating another request. Offset: 0x8004 Read/Write: See table below Parity Protection: See table below Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000007 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,x111) Bit R/W Parity Protection Reset Description RO N NOT_ACCEPTED CACTIVE: This signal indicates whether the AXI low- power request was accepted by HW or not : 1 : Not accepted, requires Clock, 0 : Accepted, Clock can be gated 0 = ACCEPTED 1 = NOT_ACCEPTED RO N DEASSERTED CSYSACK: This signal is the acknowledgment to the low- power request from the system. Active Low signal 0 = ASSERTED 1 = DEASSERTED RW Y DISABLE CSYSREQ: When this signal is low, it indicates that the system clock controller requested the AXI low power interface to enter the low-power state. When high, this signal indicates that the AXI low power interface should come out of the low-power state. 0 = ENABLE 1 = DISABLE

1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers ETHER_QOS_AUXILLARY_TIMESTAMP_0 Offset: 0x8008 Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0) Bit Reset Description DISABLE SNAPSHOT: This signal goes high to take an auxiliary snapshot of the time and store it in the auxiliary timestamp FIFO. A rising edge on this port is used to trigger the auxiliary snapshot 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE ETHER_QOS_SYNC_TSC_PTP_CAPTURE_0 TIME STAMP related Capture control and values. Write into ETHER_QOS_SYNC_TSC_PTP_CAPTURE_0 to capture the timestamp from TSC and EQOS simultaneously This bit is written to Logic 1 to start the capture of TSC and PTP (from MAC) and reset by the H/W after the capture is complete. Offset: 0x800c Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0) Bit Reset Description DONE SYNC_TSC_PTP_CAPTURE: 0 = DONE 1 = START ETHER_QOS_TSC_CAPTURE_LOW_0 Offset: 0x8010 Read/Write: RO Parity Protection: N Shadow: N

1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000) Bit Reset Description 31:0 0x0 TSC_TIMER_VALUE_LOW ETHER_QOS_TSC_CAPTURE_HIGH_0 Offset: 0x8014 Read/Write: RO Parity Protection: N Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000) Bit Reset Description 31:0 0x0 TSC_TIMER_VALUE_HIGH ETHER_QOS_PTP_CAPTURE_LOW_0 Offset: 0x8018 Read/Write: RO Parity Protection: N Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000) Bit Reset Description 31:0 0x0 PTP_TIMER_VALUE_LOW ETHER_QOS_PTP_CAPTURE_HIGH_0 Offset: 0x801c Read/Write: RO Parity Protection: N Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000) Bit Reset Description 31:0 0x0 PTP_TIMER_VALUE_HIGH

1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers ETHER_QOS_VIRTUAL_APB_CH0_DMA_CTRL_0 Adding Interrupt control and status registers for various safety errors generated from the MAC IP DMA of CH0 to CH7 can be allocated to different GuestOSes by RM through the below registers. At any given instant one channel should be allocated to a single OS`es ONLY DMA CH0 to VM Mapping. 1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers Bit Reset Description 0x0 OS0: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE ETHER_QOS_VIRTUAL_APB_CH7_DMA_CTRL_0 DMA CH7 to VM Mapping Offset: 0x821c Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000) Bit Reset Description 0x0 OS3: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 OS2: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 OS1: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 OS0: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE ETHER_QOS_VIRTUAL_APB_ERR_CTRL_0 If any OSes access CHx registers other than the one that is allocated to,this is treated as illegal and all register writes are dropped and reads are masked (0x00000000). Any illegal CHx register access would generate an APB slave error, RM can enable or disable the error propagation onto the APB bus OS5 is assigned for providing read only access to the PTP registers. 1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers Bit Reset Description DISABLE OS5: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE DISABLE OS3: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE DISABLE OS2: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE DISABLE OS1: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE DISABLE OS0: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE ETHER_QOS_VIRTUAL_APB_ERR_STATUS_0 VIRTUAL_APB_ERR_STATUS monitors the illegal CHx register access by each OSes. This bit is asserted irrespective of whether the corresponding bit in the VIRTUAL_APB_ERR_CTRL bit is set or not. 1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers Bit Reset Description 7:0 0x0 CH4 ETHER_QOS_VIRTUAL_HV_APB_ERR_CTRL_0 If RM tries to access HV registers this is treated as illegal and all register writes are dropped and reads are masked(0x00000000) if HV tries to access registers other than HV allocated set, ERR status is set. Any illegal register access would generate an APB slave error, HV can enable or disable the error propagation onto the APB bus using below ERR_CTRL register. Offset: 0x8500 Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00) Bit Reset Description DISABLE HV: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE DISABLE RM: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE ETHER_QOS_VIRTUAL_HV_APB_ERR_STATUS_0 VIRTUAL_HV_APB_ERR_STATUS monitors the illegal register access to HV page by RM. This bit is asserted irrespective of whether the corresponding bit in the VIRTUAL_HV_APB_ERR_CTRL bit is set or not. Offset: 0x8504 Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00) Bit Reset Description CLEAR HV: 0 = CLEAR 1 = ACTIVE 1 = SW_CLEAR

1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers Bit Reset Description CLEAR RM: 0 = CLEAR 1 = ACTIVE 1 = SW_CLEAR ETHER_QOS_VIRTUAL_INTR_CH0_CTRL_0 The DMA channel interrupts from CORE is actually pulse, so need to latch them and SW should be able to clear them using the WRAPPER registers. A Guest OS can access the INTR_CHx registers for the CHx that are assigned to it. Offset: 0x8600 Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00) Bit Reset Description DISABLE RX: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE DISABLE TX: 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE ETHER_QOS_VIRTUAL_INTR_CH0_STATUS_0 Offset: 0x8604 Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00) Bit Reset Description CLEAR RX: 0 = CLEAR 1 = ACTIVE 1 = SW_CLEAR CLEAR TX: 0 = CLEAR 1 = ACTIVE 1 = SW_CLEAR

1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers Bit Reset Description 0x0 COMP_PAD_E_TEST_OUT: used to control e_test_out input of COMP pad 10:7 0x0 COMP_PAD_RFU_IN: Reserved. 5:4 0x0 COMP_PAD_TEST_SEL: used to control test_sel input of COMP pad 3:0 0x7 EQOS2TMC_CFG_SDMEMCOMP_VREF_SEL: used to control vref_sel input of COMP pad Should be set appropriately before starting calibration ETHER_QOS_AUTO_CAL_CONFIG_0 SDMEMCOMP pad auto-calibration settings Offset: 0x8804 Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00010000 (0b0000,xxxx,xxxx,x001,xxx0,0000,xxx0,0000) PROD: 0x20000000 (0bxx1x,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx) Bit Reset PROD Description 0x0 _NONE_ AUTO_CAL_START: Writing a one to this bit starts the calibration state machine. This bit must be set even if the override is set in order to latch in the override value. 0x0 _NONE_ AUTO_CAL_OVERRIDE: AUTOCAL override. 0 = NORMAL :0 (normal operation): use AUTO_CAL_PU/PD_OFFSET as an offset to the calibration state machine setting 1 = OVERRIDE :1 (override) : use AUTO_CAL_PU/ PD_OFFSET register values directly DISABLED ENABLED AUTO_CAL_ENABLE: AUTOCAL enable. 0 = DISABLED :0 (disabled): use ether_qos2tmc_cfg* register settings for pullup/dn 1 = ENABLED :1 (normal operation): use EQOS generated pullup/dn (override or AUTOCAL)

ETHER_QOS_ERRCOLLATOR_SWRESET_0 Offset: 0xf004 Read/Write: WO Parity Protection: N Shadow: N

1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0) Bit Reset Description 0x0 SWRST: 1'b1 : Issue a SW reset to the Error Collator. This will reset all the registers(Except SCR), counters and logic of the Error Collator. SW can use this bit to flush errors logged into the error collator for ex, after Boot, SC7/8 exit. 1'b0 : Do nothing, reset value. This bit is auto-cleared. ETHER_QOS_ERRCOLLATOR_MISSIONERR_TYPE_0 Offset: 0xf008 Read/Write: RO Parity Protection: N Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000005 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00,0101) Bit Reset Description 5:0 0x5 CODE: This register indicates the fault code of the error line based on the value of MISSIONERR_INDEX Register. This can be used by a fault handling agent to triage an error without requiring device-specific code.The possible values of this field are: 6'd0 : None 6'd1 : Parity Error on internal data path 6'd2 : ECC SEC Error on internal data path 6'd3 : ECC DED Error on internal data path 6'd4 : Comparator Error 6'd5 : Register Parity Error 6'd6 : Parity Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd7 : ECC SEC Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd8 : ECC DED Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd9 : Clock Monitor Error 6'd10 : Voltage Error 6'd11 : Temperature Error 6'd12 : CRC Error on internal data path 6'd16 : SW Corrected Error 6'd17 : SW Uncorrected Error 6'd18 : SW Generic Error 6'd20 : ECC SED Error on internal data path 6'd21 : ECC SED Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd32 : Other HW Corrected Error 6'd33 : Other HW Uncorrected Error All other values : Reserved ETHER_QOS_ERRCOLLATOR_CURRENT_COUNTER_VALUE_0 Offset: 0xf00c

1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers Read/Write: RO Parity Protection: N Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0,0000,0000) Bit Reset Description 8:0 0x0 VALUE: Provides the current value of the counter corresponding to the error in MissionErr_Index Register. Default provides the value of error 0 counter. Bit[8] is the ovrerflow bit post which the counter saturates and does not counter further. ETHER_QOS_ERRCOLLATOR_MISSIONERR_INDEX_0 Offset: 0xf014 Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00) Bit Reset Description 1:0 0x0 IDX: BINARY Encoded. For error number 32, register should be programmed with value 0x20. Write to this register with Error number will update:
- MISSIONERR_TYPE Register with the Error-Code for the Error.
- CURRENT_COUNTER_VALUE Register with the error's SEC/DED Counter.
- MISSIONERR_USERVALUE with value of the first error_<i>_user signal.
SW can use this to trage the error. number shall update the MISSIONERR_TYPE register with the error code and the Current_Counter_Value register with the value of the errors SEC/DED counter. SW can use this register to triage the error. ETHER_QOS_ERRCOLLATOR_CORRECTABLE_THRESHOLD_0 Offset: 0xf018 Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0000)

1G Ethernet Controller QoS Registers Bit Reset Description 7:0 0x0 COUNT: Threshold value for all SEC Fault Reporting Units connected to this error collator. SEC Errors are logged once the threshold is reached and the overflow bit is set. 7'b0 : Log SEC error after receiving 1 Error. 7'b1 : Log SEC error after receiving 2 Errors. ... 7'bFF : Log SEC error after receiving 256 Errors. ETHER_QOS_ERRCOLLATOR_MISSIONERR_INJECT_UNLOCK_0 Offset: 0xf01c Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: N Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0000) Bit Reset Description 7:0 0x0 VALUE: Writes to ERRSLICE_XXX_MISSIONERR_INJECT registers are disabled until this register is written with a value of 0xE1. This is to prevent an inadvertent safety error injection in the safety plugin due to: 1. A fault on ERRSLICE_XXX_MISSIONERR_INJECT register itself. 2. Erroneous SW. The register shall be written with a value of 0x0 to reestablish the lock after user has completed the error injection testing. 0xE1 : Unlock the MISSIONERR_INJECT Register 0x0 : Lock the MISSIONERR_INJECT Register 0 = LOCK 225 = UNLOCK ETHER_QOS_ERRCOLLATOR_ERRSLICE0_MISSIONERR_ENABLE_0 Offset: 0xf030 Read/Write: R/W Parity Protection: Y Shadow: N SCR Protection: 0 Reset: 0x0000000f (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,1111)

MAC Security (MACsec)
